# <a name="troubleshoot-aspnet-core-on-azure-app-service-and-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-103">Solucionar problemas ASP.NET Core no serviço Azure App e no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-103">Troubleshoot ASP.NET Core on Azure App Service and IIS</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-110">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-110">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>](#troubleshoot-on-iis)

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-117">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-117">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-118">No Visual Studio, um projeto do ASP.NET Core usa por padrão a hospedagem do [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-118">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-119">Uma *falha de 502,5 processo* ou uma *falha de início de 500,30* que ocorre quando a depuração local pode ser diagnosticada usando o Conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-119">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-120">403,14 proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-120">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-121">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-121">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-122">O seguinte erro é registrado em log:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-122">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-123">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-123">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-124">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta incorreta no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-124">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-125">O processo de implantação não moveu todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-125">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-126">O arquivo de *web.config* está ausente na implantação ou o conteúdo do arquivo de *web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-126">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-127">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-127">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-128">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-128">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-129">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem usando o método normal de implantação, como o Visual Studio, o PowerShell ou a implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-129">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-130">Confirme se o arquivo de *web.config* está presente na implantação e se seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-130">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-131">Ao hospedar no serviço Azure App, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado na `D:\home\site\wwwroot` pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-131">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-132">Quando o aplicativo é hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **configurações básicas**do **Gerenciador do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-132">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-133">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo estão implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem ao conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-133">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-134">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core publicado, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-134">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-135">Para obter mais informações sobre o arquivo de *web.config* , consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-135">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-136">500 Erro Interno do Servidor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-136">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-137">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-137">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-138">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-138">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-139">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-139">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-140">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-140">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-141">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-141">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-142">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-142">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-143">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-143">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-144">500.0 Falha de carregamento de manipulador em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-144">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-145">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-145">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-146">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-146">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-147">Erro desconhecido ao carregar ASP.NET Core componentes do [módulo](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-147">An unknown error occurred loading [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-148">Execute uma das seguintes ações:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-148">Take one of the following actions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-149">Entre em contato com o [Suporte da Microsoft](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (selecione **Ferramentas para Desenvolvedores** e, em seguida, **ASP.NET Core**).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-149">Contact [Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (select **Developer Tools** then **ASP.NET Core**).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-150">Faça uma pergunta no Stack Overflow.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-150">Ask a question on Stack Overflow.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-151">Registre um problema no nosso [Repositório do GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-151">File an issue on our [GitHub repository](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span></span>

### <a name="50030-in-process-startup-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-152">500.30 Falha de inicialização em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-152">500.30 In-Process Startup Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-153">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-153">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-154">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-154">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-155">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o .NET Core CLR em processo, mas falha ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-155">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core CLR in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-156">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-156">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-157">Condições comuns de falha:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-157">Common failure conditions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-158">O aplicativo está configurado incorretamente devido ao direcionamento de uma versão do ASP.NET Core estrutura compartilhada que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-158">The app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-159">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-159">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-160">Usando Azure Key Vault, falta de permissões para o Key Vault.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-160">Using Azure Key Vault, lack of permissions to the Key Vault.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-161">Verifique as políticas de acesso no Key Vault de destino para garantir que as permissões corretas sejam concedidas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-161">Check the access policies in the targeted Key Vault to ensure that the correct permissions are granted.</span></span>

### <a name="50031-ancm-failed-to-find-native-dependencies"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-162">500.31 O ANCM não pôde encontrar dependências nativas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-162">500.31 ANCM Failed to Find Native Dependencies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-163">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-163">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-164">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-164">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-165">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o tempo de execução do .NET Core em processo, mas falha ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-165">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core runtime in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-166">A causa mais comum dessa falha de inicialização é quando o runtime `Microsoft.NETCore.App` ou `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` não está instalado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-166">The most common cause of this startup failure is when the `Microsoft.NETCore.App` or `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` runtime isn't installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-167">Se o aplicativo for implantado no ASP.NET Core 3.0 de destino e essa versão não existir no computador, esse erro ocorrerá.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-167">If the app is deployed to target ASP.NET Core 3.0 and that version doesn't exist on the machine, this error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-168">Segue um exemplo de mensagem de erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-168">An example error message follows:</span></span>

```
The specified framework 'Microsoft.NETCore.App', version '3.0.0' was not found.
  - The following frameworks were found:
      2.2.1 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview5-27626-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27713-13 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27714-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27723-08 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-169">A mensagem de erro lista todas as versões instaladas do .NET Core e a versão solicitada pelo aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-169">The error message lists all the installed .NET Core versions and the version requested by the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-170">Para corrigir esse erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-170">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-171">Instale a versão adequada do .NET Core no computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-171">Install the appropriate version of .NET Core on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-172">Altere o aplicativo para uma versão do .NET Core que está presente no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-172">Change the app to target a version of .NET Core that's present on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-173">Publique o aplicativo como uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-173">Publish the app as a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-174">Durante a execução no desenvolvimento (quando a variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` está definida como `Development`), o erro específico é gravado na resposta HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-174">When running in development (the `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` environment variable is set to `Development`), the specific error is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-175">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo também é encontrada no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-175">The cause of a process startup failure is also found in the Application Event Log.</span></span>

### <a name="50032-ancm-failed-to-load-dll"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-176">500.32 O ANCM não pôde carregar o dll</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-176">500.32 ANCM Failed to Load dll</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-177">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-177">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-178">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-178">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-179">A causa mais comum para esse erro é que o aplicativo foi publicado para uma arquitetura de processador incompatível.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-179">The most common cause for this error is that the app is published for an incompatible processor architecture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-180">Esse erro ocorrerá se o processo de trabalho estiver em execução como um aplicativo de 32 bits e o aplicativo tiver sido publicado para o destino de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-180">If the worker process is running as a 32-bit app and the app was published to target 64-bit, this error occurs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-181">Para corrigir esse erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-181">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-182">Republique o aplicativo para a mesma arquitetura de processador que o processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-182">Republish the app for the same processor architecture as the worker process.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-183">Publique o aplicativo como uma [implantação dependente da estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-183">Publish the app as a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span></span>

### <a name="50033-ancm-request-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-184">500.33 O ANCM não pôde carregar o manipulador de solicitação</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-184">500.33 ANCM Request Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-185">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-185">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-186">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-186">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-187">O aplicativo não referenciou a estrutura `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-187">The app didn't reference the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-188">Somente aplicativos direcionados à `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` estrutura podem ser hospedados pelo [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-188">Only apps targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework can be hosted by the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-189">Para corrigir esse erro, confirme se o aplicativo está direcionado para a estrutura `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-189">To fix this error, confirm that the app is targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-190">Confira o `.runtimeconfig.json` para verificar a estrutura de destino do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-190">Check the `.runtimeconfig.json` to verify the framework targeted by the app.</span></span>

### <a name="50034-ancm-mixed-hosting-models-not-supported"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-191">500.34 Não há suporte para modelos de hospedagem mistos do ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-191">500.34 ANCM Mixed Hosting Models Not Supported</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-192">O processo de trabalho não pode executar um aplicativo em processo e um aplicativo fora do processo no mesmo processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-192">The worker process can't run both an in-process app and an out-of-process app in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-193">Para corrigir esse erro, execute aplicativos em pools de aplicativos do IIS separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-193">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50035-ancm-multiple-in-process-applications-in-same-process"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-194">500.35 Vários aplicativos do ANCM em processo no mesmo processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-194">500.35 ANCM Multiple In-Process Applications in same Process</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-195">O processo de trabalho não pode executar vários aplicativos em processo no mesmo processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-195">The worker process can't run multiple in-process apps in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-196">Para corrigir esse erro, execute aplicativos em pools de aplicativos do IIS separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-196">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50036-ancm-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-197">500.36 Falha ao carregar o manipulador de fora do processo do ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-197">500.36 ANCM Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-198">O manipulador de solicitação de fora do processo *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* não está próximo do arquivo *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-198">The out-of-process request handler, *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll*, isn't next to the *aspnetcorev2.dll* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-199">Isso indica uma instalação corrompida do [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-199">This indicates a corrupted installation of the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-200">Para corrigir esse erro, repare a instalação do [Pacote de Hospedagem do .NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (para IIS) ou do Visual Studio (para o IIS Express).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-200">To fix this error, repair the installation of the [.NET Core Hosting Bundle](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (for IIS) or Visual Studio (for IIS Express).</span></span>

### <a name="50037-ancm-failed-to-start-within-startup-time-limit"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-201">500.37 O ANCM não pôde ser iniciado dentro do limite de tempo de inicialização</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-201">500.37 ANCM Failed to Start Within Startup Time Limit</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-202">O ANCM não pôde ser iniciado dentro do limite de tempo de inicialização fornecido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-202">ANCM failed to start within the provied startup time limit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-203">Por padrão, o tempo limite é de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-203">By default, the timeout is 120 seconds.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-204">Esse erro pode ocorrer ao iniciar um grande número de aplicativos no mesmo computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-204">This error can occur when starting a large number of apps on the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-205">Verifique se há picos de uso de CPU/memória no servidor durante a inicialização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-205">Check for CPU/Memory usage spikes on the server during startup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-206">Talvez você precise balancear o processo de inicialização de vários aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-206">You may need to stagger the startup process of multiple apps.</span></span>

### <a name="50038-ancm-application-dll-not-found"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-207">500,38 DLL do aplicativo ANCM não encontrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-207">500.38 ANCM Application DLL Not Found</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-208">ANCM falhou ao localizar a DLL do aplicativo, que deve estar ao lado do executável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-208">ANCM failed to locate the application DLL, which should be next to the executable.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-209">Esse erro ocorre ao hospedar um aplicativo empacotado como um [executável de arquivo único](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) usando o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-209">This error occurs when hosting an app packaged as a [single-file executable](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) using the in-process hosting model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-210">O modelo em processo requer que o ANCM carregue o aplicativo .NET Core no processo existente do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-210">The in-process model requires that the ANCM load the .NET Core app into the existing IIS process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-211">Esse cenário não é suportado pelo modelo de implantação de arquivo único.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-211">This scenario isn't supported by the single-file deployment model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-212">Use **uma** das seguintes abordagens no arquivo de projeto do aplicativo para corrigir esse erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-212">Use **one** of the following approaches in the app's project file to fix this error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-213">Desabilite a publicação de arquivo único definindo a `PublishSingleFile` Propriedade MSBuild como `false` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-213">Disable single-file publishing by setting the `PublishSingleFile` MSBuild property to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-214">Alterne para o modelo de hospedagem fora do processo definindo a `AspNetCoreHostingModel` Propriedade MSBuild como `OutOfProcess` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-214">Switch to the out-of-process hosting model by setting the `AspNetCoreHostingModel` MSBuild property to `OutOfProcess`.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-215">502.5 Falha de processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-215">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-216">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-216">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-217">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-217">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-218">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-218">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-219">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-219">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-220">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-220">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-221">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-221">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-222">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll*) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-222">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-223">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-223">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-224">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-224">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-225">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-225">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-226">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-226">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-227">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo (*.dll*) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-227">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-228">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-228">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-229">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-229">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-230">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-230">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-231">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-231">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-232">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-232">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-233">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-233">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-234">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-234">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-235">Confirme se não há um conflito entre uma `<Platform>` Propriedade do MSBuild no arquivo de projeto e o bit de bits publicado do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-235">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-236">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-236">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-237">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-237">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-238">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-238">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-239">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-239">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-240">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-240">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-241">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-241">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-242">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com um *startupTimeLimit* padrão de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-242">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-243">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-243">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-244">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-244">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-245">Solucionar problemas no serviço Azure App</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-245">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-246">Log de eventos do aplicativo (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-246">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-247">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-247">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-248">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-248">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-249">Selecione **Diagnóstico e solução de problemas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-249">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-250">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-250">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-251">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte**, selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-251">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-252">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-252">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-253">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-253">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-254">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-254">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-255">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-255">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-256">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-256">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-257">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-257">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-258">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-258">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-259">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-259">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-260">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-260">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-261">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-261">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-262">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-262">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-263">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-263">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-264">Você pode executar o aplicativo no Console de Execução Remota do [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) para descobrir o erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-264">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-265">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-265">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-266">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-266">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-267">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-267">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-268">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-268">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-269">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-269">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-270">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-270">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-271">Executar o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-271">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-272">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-272">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-273">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-273">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-274">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-274">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-275">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-275">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-276">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-276">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-277">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-277">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-278">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-278">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-279">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-279">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-292">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-292">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-293">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-293">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-294">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-294">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-295">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-295">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-296">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA**, selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-296">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-297">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout**, selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-297">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-298">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-298">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-299">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-299">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-300">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-300">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-301">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-301">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-302">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-302">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-303">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-303">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-304">Volte para o portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-304">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-305">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-305">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-306">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-306">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-307">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-307">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-308">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-308">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-309">Abra a pasta **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-309">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-310">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-310">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-311">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-311">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-312">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-312">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-313">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-313">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-314">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-314">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-315">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-315">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-316">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-316">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-317">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-317">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-318">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-318">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-319">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-319">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-320">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-320">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-321">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-321">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-322">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-322">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-323">Log de depuração do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-323">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-324">O log de depuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core fornece registro em log adicional e mais profundo do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-324">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-325">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-325">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-326">Para habilitar o log de diagnóstico avançado, execute um destes procedimentos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-326">To enable the enhanced diagnostic log, perform either of the following:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-327">Siga as instruções em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) para configurar o aplicativo para um log de diagnósticos avançado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-327">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-328">Reimplante o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-328">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-329">Adicione a `<handlerSettings>` mostrada em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) para o arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo ao vivo usando o console do Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-329">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-330">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-330">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-331">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-331">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-332">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-332">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-333">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-333">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-334">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-334">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-335">Edite o arquivo *web.config* selecionando o botão de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-335">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-336">Adicione a seção `<handlerSettings>` conforme mostrado em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-336">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-337">Selecione o botão **Salvar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-337">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-338">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-338">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-339">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-339">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-340">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-340">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-341">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-341">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-342">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-342">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-343">Se você não fornecer um caminho para o arquivo *aspnetcore-debug.log*, o arquivo aparecerá na lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-343">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-344">Se você tiver fornecido um caminho, navegue até o local do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-344">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-345">Abra o arquivo de log com o botão de lápis ao lado do nome do arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-345">Open the log file with the pencil button next to the file name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-346">Desabilite o registro em log de depuração quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-346">Disable debug logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-347">Para desabilitar o log de depuração avançado, execute um destes procedimentos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-347">To disable the enhanced debug log, perform either of the following:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-348">Remova o `<handlerSettings>` do arquivo *web.config* localmente e reimplante o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-348">Remove the `<handlerSettings>` from the *web.config* file locally and redeploy the app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-349">Use o console do Kudu para editar o arquivo *web.config* e remover a seção `<handlerSettings>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-349">Use the Kudu console to edit the *web.config* file and remove the `<handlerSettings>` section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-350">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-350">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-351">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-351">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-352">A falha ao desabilitar o log de depuração pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-352">Failure to disable the debug log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-353">Não há nenhum limite no tamanho do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-353">There's no limit on log file size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-354">Somente use o log de depuração para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-354">Only use debug logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-355">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-355">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-356">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-356">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-357">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (serviço de Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-357">Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-358">Para saber mais sobre quando um aplicativo responde lentamente ou trava em uma solicitação, confira os seguintes artigos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-358">When an app responds slowly or hangs on a request, see the following articles:</span></span>
