* [<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-360">Use a Extensão de Site do Diagnosticador de Falhas para capturar o despejo para problemas de exceção intermitentes ou problemas de desempenho no aplicativo Web do Azure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-360">Use Crash Diagnoser Site Extension to Capture Dump for Intermittent Exception issues or performance issues on Azure Web App</span></span>](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/asiatech/2015/12/28/use-crash-diagnoser-site-extension-to-capture-dump-for-intermittent-exception-issues-or-performance-issues-on-azure-web-app/)

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-361">Folhas de monitoramento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-361">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-362">As folhas de monitoramento fornecem uma experiência alternativa de solução de problemas para os métodos descritos anteriormente no tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-362">Monitoring blades provide an alternative troubleshooting experience to the methods described earlier in the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-363">Essas folhas podem ser usadas para diagnosticar erros da série 500.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-363">These blades can be used to diagnose 500-series errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-364">Verifique se as Extensões do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-364">Confirm that the ASP.NET Core Extensions are installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-365">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, instale-as manualmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-365">If the extensions aren't installed, install them manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-366">Na seção de folha **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**, selecione a folha **Extensões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-366">In the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** blade section, select the **Extensions** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-367">As **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** devem aparecer na lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-367">The **ASP.NET Core Extensions** should appear in the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-368">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, selecione o botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-368">If the extensions aren't installed, select the **Add** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-369">Escolha as **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-369">Choose the **ASP.NET Core Extensions** from the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-370">Selecione **OK** para aceitar os termos legais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-370">Select **OK** to accept the legal terms.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-371">Selecione **OK** na folha **Adicionar extensão**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-371">Select **OK** on the **Add extension** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-372">Uma mensagem pop-up informativa indica quando as extensões são instaladas com êxito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-372">An informational pop-up message indicates when the extensions are successfully installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-373">Se o registro em log de stdout não estiver habilitado, siga estas etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-373">If stdout logging isn't enabled, follow these steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-374">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-374">In the Azure portal, select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-375">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-375">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-376">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-376">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-377">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-377">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-378">Abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot** e role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-378">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** and scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-379">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-379">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-380">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-380">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-381">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-381">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-382">Prossiga para ativar o log de diagnóstico:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-382">Proceed to activate diagnostic logging:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-383">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Logs de diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-383">In the Azure portal, select the **Diagnostics logs** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-384">Selecione a opção **Ligado** para **Log de Aplicativo (Sistema de arquivos)** e **Mensagens de erro detalhadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-384">Select the **On** switch for **Application Logging (Filesystem)** and **Detailed error messages**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-385">Selecione o botão **Salvar** na parte superior da folha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-385">Select the **Save** button at the top of the blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-386">Para incluir o rastreamento de solicitação com falha, também conhecido como FREB (Buffer de Evento de Solicitação com Falha), selecione a opção **Ligado** para o **Rastreamento de solicitação com falha**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-386">To include failed request tracing, also known as Failed Request Event Buffering (FREB) logging, select the **On** switch for **Failed request tracing**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-387">Selecione a folha **Fluxo de log**, que é listada imediatamente sob a folha **Logs de diagnóstico** no portal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-387">Select the **Log stream** blade, which is listed immediately under the **Diagnostics logs** blade in the portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-388">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-388">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-389">Dentro dos dados de fluxo de log, a causa do erro é indicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-389">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-390">Sempre desabilite o registro em log de stdout após concluir a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-390">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-391">Para exibir os logs de rastreamento de solicitação com falha (logs FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-391">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-392">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-392">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-393">Selecione **Logs de Rastreamento de Solicitação com Falha** da área **FERRAMENTAS DE SUPORTE** da barra lateral.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-393">Select **Failed Request Tracing Logs** from the **SUPPORT TOOLS** area of the sidebar.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-394">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-394">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-395">Para obter mais informações, veja [Habilitar log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-395">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-396">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-396">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-397">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-397">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-398">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-398">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-399">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-399">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-400">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-400">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-401">Log de eventos do aplicativo (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-401">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-402">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-402">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-403">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure *Visualizador de eventos*e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de eventos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-403">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-404">No **Visualizador de Eventos**, abra o nó **Logs do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-404">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-405">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-405">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-406">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-406">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-407">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-407">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-408">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-408">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-409">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-409">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-410">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-410">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-411">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-411">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-412">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-412">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-413">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-413">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-414">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-414">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-415">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-415">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-416">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-416">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-417">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-417">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-418">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-418">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-419">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-419">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-420">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-420">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-421">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-421">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-422">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-422">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-423">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-423">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-424">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-424">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-425">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-425">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-426">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-426">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-427">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-427">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-428">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-428">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-429">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-429">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-430">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-430">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-431">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-431">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-432">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-432">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-433">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-433">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-434">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-434">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-435">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-435">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-436">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-436">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-437">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-437">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-438">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-438">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-439">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-439">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-440">Navegue até a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-440">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-441">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-441">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-442">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-442">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-443">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-443">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-444">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-444">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-445">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-445">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-446">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-446">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-447">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-447">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-448">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-448">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-449">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-449">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-450">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-450">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-451">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-451">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-452">Log de depuração do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-452">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-453">Adicione as seguintes configurações de manipulador ao arquivo de *web.config* do aplicativo para habilitar ASP.NET Core log de depuração do módulo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-453">Add the following handler settings to the app's *web.config* file to enable ASP.NET Core Module debug log:</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore ...>
  <handlerSettings>
    <handlerSetting name="debugLevel" value="file" />
    <handlerSetting name="debugFile" value="c:\temp\ancm.log" />
  </handlerSettings>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-454">Confirme se o caminho especificado para o log existe e se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação no local.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-454">Confirm that the path specified for the log exists and that the app pool's identity has write permissions to the location.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-455">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-455">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-456">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-456">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-457">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-457">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-458">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-458">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout"
      hostingModel="InProcess">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-459">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-459">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-460">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-460">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-461">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config*, confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-461">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-462">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-462">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-463">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-463">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-464">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-464">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-465">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-465">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-466">Um *despejo* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, de inicialização ou de um aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-466">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-467">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-467">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-468">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-468">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-469">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-469">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-470">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-470">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-471">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-471">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-472">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-472">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-473">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-473">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-474">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-474">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-475">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-475">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-476">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-476">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-477">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-477">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-478">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-478">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-479">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-479">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-480">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-480">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-481">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-481">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-482">Quando um aplicativo *paralisa* (para de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [arquivos de despejo no modo de usuário: escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o despejo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-482">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-483">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-483">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-484">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-484">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-485">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-485">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-486">Limpar caches de pacote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-486">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-487">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após a atualização do SDK do .NET Core no computador de desenvolvimento ou a alteração das versões do pacote no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-487">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-488">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-488">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-489">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-489">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-490">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-490">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-491">Limpe os caches de pacote executando [dotnet NuGet local All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-491">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-492">Limpar caches de pacote também pode ser feito com a ferramenta de [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executar o comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-492">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-493">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-493">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-494">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-494">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-495">Exclua todos os arquivos na pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-495">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-526">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-526">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-527">No Visual Studio, um projeto do ASP.NET Core usa por padrão a hospedagem do [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-527">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-528">Uma *falha de 502,5 processo* ou uma *falha de início de 500,30* que ocorre quando a depuração local pode ser diagnosticada usando o Conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-528">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-529">403,14 proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-529">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-530">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-530">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-531">O seguinte erro é registrado em log:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-531">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-532">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-532">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-533">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta incorreta no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-533">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-534">O processo de implantação não moveu todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-534">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-535">O arquivo de *web.config* está ausente na implantação ou o conteúdo do arquivo de *web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-535">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-536">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-536">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-537">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-537">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-538">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem usando o método normal de implantação, como o Visual Studio, o PowerShell ou a implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-538">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-539">Confirme se o arquivo de *web.config* está presente na implantação e se seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-539">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-540">Ao hospedar no serviço Azure App, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado na `D:\home\site\wwwroot` pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-540">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-541">Quando o aplicativo é hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **configurações básicas**do **Gerenciador do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-541">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-542">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo estão implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem ao conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-542">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-543">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core publicado, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-543">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-544">Para obter mais informações sobre o arquivo de *web.config* , consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-544">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-545">500 Erro Interno do Servidor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-545">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-546">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-546">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-547">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-547">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-548">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-548">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-549">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-549">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-550">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-550">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-551">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-551">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-552">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-552">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-553">500.0 Falha de carregamento de manipulador em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-553">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-554">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-554">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-555">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-555">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-556">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) falha ao localizar o .NET Core CLR e localizar o manipulador de solicitação em processo (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-556">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the .NET Core CLR and find the in-process request handler (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-557">Verifique se:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-557">Check that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-558">O aplicativo destina-se ao pacote NuGet [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) ou ao [metapacote Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-558">The app targets either the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) NuGet package or the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-559">A versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core a que o aplicativo se destina está instalada no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-559">The version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that the app targets is installed on the target machine.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-560">500.0 Falha de carregamento de manipulador fora de processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-560">500.0 Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-561">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-561">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-562">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-562">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-563">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) falha ao localizar o manipulador de solicitação de hospedagem fora do processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-563">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the out-of-process hosting request handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-564">Verifique se a *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* está presente em uma subpasta próxima a *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-564">Make sure the *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* is present in a subfolder next to *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-565">502.5 Falha de processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-565">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-566">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-566">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-567">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-567">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-568">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-568">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-569">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-569">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-570">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-570">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-571">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-571">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-572">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll*) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-572">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-573">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-573">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-574">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-574">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-575">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-575">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-576">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-576">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-577">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo (*.dll*) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-577">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-578">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-578">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-579">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-579">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-580">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-580">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-581">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-581">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-582">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-582">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-583">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-583">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-584">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-584">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-585">Confirme se não há um conflito entre uma `<Platform>` Propriedade do MSBuild no arquivo de projeto e o bit de bits publicado do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-585">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-586">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-586">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-587">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-587">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-588">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-588">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-589">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-589">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-590">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-590">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-591">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-591">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-592">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com um *startupTimeLimit* padrão de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-592">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-593">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-593">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-594">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-594">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-595">Solucionar problemas no serviço Azure App</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-595">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-596">Log de eventos do aplicativo (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-596">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-597">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-597">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-598">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-598">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-599">Selecione **Diagnóstico e solução de problemas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-599">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-600">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-600">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-601">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte**, selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-601">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-602">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-602">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-603">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-603">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-604">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-604">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-605">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-605">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-606">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-606">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-607">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-607">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-608">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-608">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-609">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-609">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-610">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-610">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-611">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-611">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-612">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-612">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-619">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-619">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-620">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-620">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-621">Executar o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-621">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-622">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-622">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-623">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-623">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-624">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-624">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-625">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-625">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-626">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-626">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-627">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-627">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-628">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-628">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-629">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-629">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-630">Testar um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-630">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-631">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-631">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-632">Se o aplicativo for uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) de 64 bits (x64):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-632">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-633">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-633">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-635">Execute o aplicativo: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-635">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-636">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-636">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-637">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-637">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>
