### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-642">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-642">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-643">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-643">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-644">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-644">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-645">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-645">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-646">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA**, selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-646">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-647">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout**, selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-647">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-648">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-648">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-649">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-649">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-650">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-650">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-651">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-651">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-652">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-652">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-653">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-653">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-654">Volte para o portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-654">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-655">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-655">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-656">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-656">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-657">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-657">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-658">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-658">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-659">Abra a pasta **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-659">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-660">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-660">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-661">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-661">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-662">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-662">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-663">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-663">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-664">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-664">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-665">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-665">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-666">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-666">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-667">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-667">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-668">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-668">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-669">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-669">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-670">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-670">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-671">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-671">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-672">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-672">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-673">Log de depuração do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-673">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-674">O log de depuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core fornece registro em log adicional e mais profundo do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-674">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-675">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-675">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-677">Siga as instruções em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) para configurar o aplicativo para um log de diagnósticos avançado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-677">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-678">Reimplante o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-678">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-679">Adicione a `<handlerSettings>` mostrada em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) para o arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo ao vivo usando o console do Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-679">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-680">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-680">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-681">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-681">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-682">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-682">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-683">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-683">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-684">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-684">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-685">Edite o arquivo *web.config* selecionando o botão de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-685">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-686">Adicione a seção `<handlerSettings>` conforme mostrado em [Logs de diagnóstico avançados](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-686">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-687">Selecione o botão **Salvar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-687">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-688">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-688">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-689">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-689">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-690">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-690">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-692">Abra as pastas no caminho **site**  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-692">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-693">Se você não fornecer um caminho para o arquivo *aspnetcore-debug.log*, o arquivo aparecerá na lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-693">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-694">Se você tiver fornecido um caminho, navegue até o local do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-694">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-711">Folhas de monitoramento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-711">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-712">As folhas de monitoramento fornecem uma experiência alternativa de solução de problemas para os métodos descritos anteriormente no tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-712">Monitoring blades provide an alternative troubleshooting experience to the methods described earlier in the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-713">Essas folhas podem ser usadas para diagnosticar erros da série 500.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-713">These blades can be used to diagnose 500-series errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-714">Verifique se as Extensões do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-714">Confirm that the ASP.NET Core Extensions are installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-715">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, instale-as manualmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-715">If the extensions aren't installed, install them manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-716">Na seção de folha **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**, selecione a folha **Extensões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-716">In the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** blade section, select the **Extensions** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-717">As **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** devem aparecer na lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-717">The **ASP.NET Core Extensions** should appear in the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-718">Se as extensões não estiverem instaladas, selecione o botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-718">If the extensions aren't installed, select the **Add** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-719">Escolha as **Extensões do ASP.NET Core** da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-719">Choose the **ASP.NET Core Extensions** from the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-720">Selecione **OK** para aceitar os termos legais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-720">Select **OK** to accept the legal terms.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-721">Selecione **OK** na folha **Adicionar extensão**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-721">Select **OK** on the **Add extension** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-722">Uma mensagem pop-up informativa indica quando as extensões são instaladas com êxito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-722">An informational pop-up message indicates when the extensions are successfully installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-723">Se o registro em log de stdout não estiver habilitado, siga estas etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-723">If stdout logging isn't enabled, follow these steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-724">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-724">In the Azure portal, select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-725">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-725">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-726">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-726">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-727">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-727">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-728">Abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot** e role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-728">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** and scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-729">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-729">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-730">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-730">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-731">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-731">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-732">Prossiga para ativar o log de diagnóstico:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-732">Proceed to activate diagnostic logging:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-733">No portal do Azure, selecione a folha **Logs de diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-733">In the Azure portal, select the **Diagnostics logs** blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-734">Selecione a opção **Ligado** para **Log de Aplicativo (Sistema de arquivos)** e **Mensagens de erro detalhadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-734">Select the **On** switch for **Application Logging (Filesystem)** and **Detailed error messages**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-735">Selecione o botão **Salvar** na parte superior da folha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-735">Select the **Save** button at the top of the blade.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-736">Para incluir o rastreamento de solicitação com falha, também conhecido como FREB (Buffer de Evento de Solicitação com Falha), selecione a opção **Ligado** para o **Rastreamento de solicitação com falha**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-736">To include failed request tracing, also known as Failed Request Event Buffering (FREB) logging, select the **On** switch for **Failed request tracing**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-737">Selecione a folha **Fluxo de log**, que é listada imediatamente sob a folha **Logs de diagnóstico** no portal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-737">Select the **Log stream** blade, which is listed immediately under the **Diagnostics logs** blade in the portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-738">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-738">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-739">Dentro dos dados de fluxo de log, a causa do erro é indicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-739">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-740">Sempre desabilite o registro em log de stdout após concluir a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-740">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-741">Para exibir os logs de rastreamento de solicitação com falha (logs FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-741">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-742">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-742">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-743">Selecione **Logs de Rastreamento de Solicitação com Falha** da área **FERRAMENTAS DE SUPORTE** da barra lateral.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-743">Select **Failed Request Tracing Logs** from the **SUPPORT TOOLS** area of the sidebar.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-744">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-744">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-745">Para obter mais informações, veja [Habilitar log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-745">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-746">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-746">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-747">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-747">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-748">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-748">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-749">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-749">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-750">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-750">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-751">Log de eventos do aplicativo (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-751">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-752">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-752">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-753">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure *Visualizador de eventos*e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de eventos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-753">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-754">No **Visualizador de Eventos**, abra o nó **Logs do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-754">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-755">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-755">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-756">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-756">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-757">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-757">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-758">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-758">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-759">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-759">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-760">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-760">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-761">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-761">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-762">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-762">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-763">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-763">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-764">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-764">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-765">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-765">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-766">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-766">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-767">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-767">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-768">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-768">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-769">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-769">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-770">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-770">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-771">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-771">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-772">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-772">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-773">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-773">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-774">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-774">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-775">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-775">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-776">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-776">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-777">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-777">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-778">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-778">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-779">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-779">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-780">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-780">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-781">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-781">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-782">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-782">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-783">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-783">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-784">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-784">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-785">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-785">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-786">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-786">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-787">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-787">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-788">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-788">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-789">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-789">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-790">Navegue até a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-790">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-791">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-791">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-792">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-792">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-793">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-793">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-794">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-794">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-795">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-795">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-796">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-796">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-797">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-797">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-798">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-798">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-799">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-799">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-800">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-800">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-801">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-801">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-802">Log de depuração do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-802">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-803">Adicione as seguintes configurações de manipulador ao arquivo de *web.config* do aplicativo para habilitar ASP.NET Core log de depuração do módulo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-803">Add the following handler settings to the app's *web.config* file to enable ASP.NET Core Module debug log:</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore ...>
  <handlerSettings>
    <handlerSetting name="debugLevel" value="file" />
    <handlerSetting name="debugFile" value="c:\temp\ancm.log" />
  </handlerSettings>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-804">Confirme se o caminho especificado para o log existe e se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação no local.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-804">Confirm that the path specified for the log exists and that the app pool's identity has write permissions to the location.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-805">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-805">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-806">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-806">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-807">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-807">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-808">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-808">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout"
      hostingModel="InProcess">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-809">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-809">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-810">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-810">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-811">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config*, confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-811">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-812">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-812">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-813">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-813">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-814">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-814">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-815">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-815">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-816">Um *despejo* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, de inicialização ou de um aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-816">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-817">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-817">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-818">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-818">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-819">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-819">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-820">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-820">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-821">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-821">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-822">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-822">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-823">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-823">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-824">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-824">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-825">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-825">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-826">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-826">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-827">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-827">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-828">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-828">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-829">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-829">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-830">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-830">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-831">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-831">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-832">Quando um aplicativo *paralisa* (para de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [arquivos de despejo no modo de usuário: escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o despejo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-832">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-833">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-833">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-834">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-834">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-835">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-835">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-836">Limpar caches de pacote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-836">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-837">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após a atualização do SDK do .NET Core no computador de desenvolvimento ou a alteração das versões do pacote no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-837">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-838">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-838">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-839">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-839">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-840">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-840">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-841">Limpe os caches de pacote executando [dotnet NuGet local All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-841">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-842">Limpar caches de pacote também pode ser feito com a ferramenta de [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executar o comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-842">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-843">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-843">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-844">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-844">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-845">Exclua todos os arquivos na pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-845">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>
