## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-876">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-876">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-877">No Visual Studio, um projeto do ASP.NET Core usa por padrão a hospedagem do [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-877">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-878">Uma *falha de processo 502,5* que ocorre ao depurar localmente pode ser diagnosticada usando o Conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-878">A *502.5 Process Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-879">403,14 proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-879">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-880">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-880">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-881">O seguinte erro é registrado em log:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-881">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-882">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-882">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-883">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta incorreta no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-883">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-884">O processo de implantação não moveu todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-884">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-885">O arquivo de *web.config* está ausente na implantação ou o conteúdo do arquivo de *web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-885">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-886">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-886">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-887">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-887">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-888">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem usando o método normal de implantação, como o Visual Studio, o PowerShell ou a implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-888">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-889">Confirme se o arquivo de *web.config* está presente na implantação e se seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-889">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-890">Ao hospedar no serviço Azure App, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado na `D:\home\site\wwwroot` pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-890">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-891">Quando o aplicativo é hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **configurações básicas**do **Gerenciador do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-891">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-892">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo estão implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem ao conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-892">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-893">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core publicado, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-893">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-894">Para obter mais informações sobre o arquivo de *web.config* , consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-894">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-895">500 Erro Interno do Servidor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-895">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-896">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-896">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-897">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-897">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-898">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-898">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-899">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-899">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-900">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-900">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-901">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-901">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-902">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-902">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-903">502.5 Falha de processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-903">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-904">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-904">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-905">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-905">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-906">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-906">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-907">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-907">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-908">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-908">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-909">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-909">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-910">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll*) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-910">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-911">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-911">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-912">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-912">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-913">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-913">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-914">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-914">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-915">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo (*.dll*) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-915">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-916">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-916">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-917">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-917">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-918">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-918">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-919">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-919">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-920">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-920">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-921">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-921">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-922">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-922">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-923">Confirme se não há um conflito entre uma `<Platform>` Propriedade do MSBuild no arquivo de projeto e o bit de bits publicado do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-923">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-924">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-924">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-925">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-925">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-926">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-926">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-927">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-927">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-928">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-928">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-929">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-929">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-930">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com um *startupTimeLimit* padrão de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-930">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-931">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-931">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-932">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-932">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-933">Solucionar problemas no serviço Azure App</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-933">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-934">Log de eventos do aplicativo (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-934">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-935">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-935">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-936">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-936">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-937">Selecione **Diagnóstico e solução de problemas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-937">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-938">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-938">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-939">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte**, selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-939">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-940">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-940">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-941">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-941">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-942">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-942">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-943">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-943">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-944">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-944">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-945">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-945">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-946">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-946">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-947">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-947">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-948">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-948">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-949">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-949">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-950">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-950">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-951">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-951">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-952">Você pode executar o aplicativo no Console de Execução Remota do [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) para descobrir o erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-952">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-953">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-953">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-954">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-954">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-955">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-955">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-956">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-956">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-957">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-957">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-958">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-958">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-959">Executar o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-959">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-960">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-960">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-961">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-961">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-962">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-962">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-963">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-963">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-964">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-964">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-965">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-965">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-966">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-966">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-967">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-967">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-968">Testar um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-968">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-969">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-969">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-970">Se o aplicativo for uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) de 64 bits (x64):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-970">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\Program Files\dotnet`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-971">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-971">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-972">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-972">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-973">Execute o aplicativo: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-973">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-974">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-974">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-975">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-975">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-976">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-976">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-977">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-977">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-978">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-978">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-979">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é conectada ao console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-979">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-980">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-980">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-981">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-981">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-982">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-982">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-983">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-983">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-984">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA**, selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-984">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-985">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout**, selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-985">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-986">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-986">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-987">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-987">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-988">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-988">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-989">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-989">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-990">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-990">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-991">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-991">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-992">Volte para o portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-992">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-993">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-993">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-994">Selecione o botão **Ir&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-994">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-995">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-995">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-996">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-996">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-997">Abra a pasta **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-997">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-998">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-998">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-999">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-999">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1000">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1000">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1001">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1001">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1002">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1002">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1003">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1003">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1004">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1004">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1005">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1005">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1006">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1006">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1007">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1007">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1008">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1008">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1009">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1009">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1010">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1010">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1043">Dentro dos dados de fluxo de log, a causa do erro é indicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1043">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1048">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1048">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1049">Para obter mais informações, veja [Habilitar log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1049">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1052">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1052">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1053">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1053">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1054">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1054">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1055">Log de eventos do aplicativo (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1055">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1056">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1056">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1057">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure *Visualizador de eventos*e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de eventos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1057">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1058">No **Visualizador de Eventos**, abra o nó **Logs do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1058">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1059">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1059">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1060">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1060">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1061">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1061">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1062">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1062">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1063">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1063">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1064">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1064">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1065">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1065">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1066">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1066">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1067">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1067">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1068">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1068">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1069">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1069">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1070">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1070">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1071">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1071">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1072">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1072">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1073">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1073">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1074">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1074">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1075">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1075">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1076">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1076">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1077">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1077">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1078">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1078">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1079">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1079">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1080">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1080">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1081">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1081">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1082">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1082">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1083">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1083">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1084">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1084">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1085">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1085">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1086">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1086">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1087">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1087">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1088">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1088">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1089">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1089">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1090">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1090">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1091">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1091">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1092">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1092">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1093">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1093">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1094">Navegue até a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1094">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1095">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1095">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1096">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1096">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1097">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1097">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1098">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1098">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1099">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1099">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1100">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1100">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1101">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1101">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1102">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1102">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1103">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1103">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1104">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1104">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1105">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1105">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1106">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1106">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1107">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1107">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1108">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1108">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1109">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1109">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1110">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1110">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1111">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config*, confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1111">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1112">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1112">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1113">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1113">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1114">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1114">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1115">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1115">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1116">Um *despejo* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, de inicialização ou de um aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1116">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1117">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1117">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1118">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1118">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1119">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1119">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1120">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1120">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1121">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1121">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1122">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1122">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1123">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1123">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1124">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1124">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1125">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1125">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1126">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1126">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1127">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1127">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1128">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1128">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1129">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1129">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1130">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1130">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1131">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1131">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1132">Quando um aplicativo *paralisa* (para de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [arquivos de despejo no modo de usuário: escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o despejo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1132">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1133">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1133">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1134">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1134">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1135">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1135">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1136">Limpar caches de pacote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1136">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1137">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após a atualização do SDK do .NET Core no computador de desenvolvimento ou a alteração das versões do pacote no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1137">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1138">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1138">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1139">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1139">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1140">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1140">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1141">Limpe os caches de pacote executando [dotnet NuGet local All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1141">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1142">Limpar caches de pacote também pode ser feito com a ferramenta de [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executar o comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1142">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1143">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1143">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1144">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1144">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="9cdfb-1145">Exclua todos os arquivos na pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9cdfb-1145">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>
